SELECT   f.id, f.ra as F_ra, f.dec as F_dec, p.ra, p.dec into mydb.MyTable from MyDB.FIRST_Reduced_#p0#deg AS f    OUTER APPLY dbo.fGetNearestObjEq(f.ra, f.dec, #) AS x     JOIN PhotoObjAll p ON x.objID = p.objID
SELECT   f.id, f.ra as F_ra, f.dec as F_dec ,p.ra, p.dec  FROM MyDB.FIRST_Reduced_#p0#deg AS f    OUTER APPLY dbo.fGetNearestObjEq(f.ra, f.dec, #) AS x     JOIN PhotoObjAll p ON x.objID = p.objID
SELECT   f.id, f.ra as F_ra, f.dec as F.dec ,p.ra, p.dec  FROM MyDB.FIRST_Reduced_#p0#deg AS f    OUTER APPLY dbo.fGetNearestObjEq(f.ra, f.dec, #) AS x     JOIN PhotoObjAll p ON x.objID = p.objID
SELECT   p.ra, p.dec  FROM MyDB.FIRST_Reduced_#p0#deg AS f    OUTER APPLY dbo.fGetNearestObjEq(f.ra, f.dec, #) AS x     JOIN PhotoObjAll p ON x.objID = p.objID
